<p><br/>
The following is a list of <b>notable deaths in November 2015</b>.</p>
<p>Entries for each day are listed <u>alphabetically</u> by surname. A typical entry lists information in the following sequence:</p>
<ul>
<li>Name, age, country of citizenship and reason for notability, established cause of death, reference.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="November_2015">November 2015</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_November_2015&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: November 2015">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1">1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_November_2015&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Abdikarim_Yusuf_Adam" title="Abdikarim Yusuf Adam">Abdikarim Yusuf Adam</a>, Somali military officer, <a href="/wiki/Somali_Armed_Forces" title="Somali Armed Forces">Chief of Army</a> (2015), shot.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bill_Ballantine_(biologist)" title="Bill Ballantine (biologist)">Bill Ballantine</a>, 78, British-born New Zealand marine biologist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Desruelles" title="Ronald Desruelles">Ronald Desruelles</a>, 60, Belgian athlete, suicide by hanging.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Thomas_R._Fitzgerald_(judge)" title="Thomas R. Fitzgerald (judge)">Thomas R. Fitzgerald</a>, 74, American judge, Chief Justice (2008–2010) and member (2000–2010) of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Illinois_Supreme_Court" title="Illinois Supreme Court">Illinois Supreme Court</a>, Parkinson's disease.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Fonseca_e_Costa" title="José Fonseca e Costa">José Fonseca e Costa</a>, 82, Portuguese film director (<i><a href="/wiki/No_Trace_of_Sin" title="No Trace of Sin">No Trace of Sin</a></i>), pneumonia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Anselmo_Gouthier" title="Anselmo Gouthier">Anselmo Gouthier</a>, 82, Italian politician.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gloria_Salguero_Gross" title="Gloria Salguero Gross">Gloria Salguero Gross</a>, 74, Salvadoran politician, President of the <a href="/wiki/Legislative_Assembly_of_El_Salvador" title="Legislative Assembly of El Salvador">Legislative Assembly</a> (1994–1997), cardiac arrest.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Stephen_Hancock" title="Stephen Hancock">Stephen Hancock</a>, 89, English actor (<i><a href="/wiki/Coronation_Street" title="Coronation Street">Coronation Street</a></i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Afzal_Khan_Lala" title="Afzal Khan Lala">Afzal Khan Lala</a>, 89, Pakistani politician, <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Pakistan" title="Parliament of Pakistan">MP</a> for <a href="/wiki/Swat_District" title="Swat District">Swat</a> (1993–1997), complications from cirrhosis.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Houston_McTear" title="Houston McTear">Houston McTear</a>, 58, American sprinter, lung cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Charles_Duncan_Michener" title="Charles Duncan Michener">Charles Duncan Michener</a>, 97, American entomologist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brijmohan_Lall_Munjal" title="Brijmohan Lall Munjal">Brijmohan Lall Munjal</a>, 92, Indian transportation manufacturing executive, co-founder of <a href="/wiki/Hero_Cycles" title="Hero Cycles">Hero Cycles</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hero_MotoCorp" title="Hero MotoCorp">Hero MotoCorp</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/G%C3%BCnter_Schabowski" title="Günter Schabowski">Günter Schabowski</a>, 86, German politician, editor-in-chief of <i><a href="/wiki/Neues_Deutschland" title="Neues Deutschland">Neues Deutschland</a></i>, First Secretary of the <a href="/wiki/East_Berlin" title="East Berlin">East Berlin</a> <a href="/wiki/Socialist_Unity_Party_of_Germany" title="Socialist Unity Party of Germany">SED</a>, prematurely announced the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fall_of_the_Berlin_Wall" title="Fall of the Berlin Wall">fall of the Berlin Wall</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hayden_Shell" title="Hayden Shell">Hayden Shell</a>, 78, Australian politician, member of the <a href="/wiki/Victorian_Legislative_Assembly" title="Victorian Legislative Assembly">Victorian Legislative Assembly</a> for <a href="/wiki/Electoral_district_of_Geelong_West" title="Electoral district of Geelong West">Geelong West</a> (1982–85) and <a href="/wiki/Electoral_district_of_Geelong" title="Electoral district of Geelong">Geelong</a> (1985–92).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rudolf_Scheurer" title="Rudolf Scheurer">Rudolf Scheurer</a>, 90, Swiss football referee.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fred_Thompson" title="Fred Thompson">Fred Thompson</a>, 73, American politician and actor (<i><a href="/wiki/Law_%26_Order" title="Law &amp; Order">Law &amp; Order</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Sinister_(film)" title="Sinister (film)">Sinister</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Cape_Fear_(1991_film)" title="Cape Fear (1991 film)">Cape Fear</a></i>), <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">U.S. Senator</a> from <a href="/wiki/Tennessee" title="Tennessee">Tennessee</a> (1994–2003), minority counsel to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senate_Watergate_Committee" title="Senate Watergate Committee">Senate Watergate Committee</a>, lymphoma.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/A._Veluppillai" title="A. Veluppillai">A. Veluppillai</a>, 78, Sri Lankan Tamil academic and author.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2">2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_November_2015&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Frank_Budgen_(director)" title="Frank Budgen (director)">Frank Budgen</a>, 61, British commercial director (<i><a href="/wiki/Tag_(advertisement)" title="Tag (advertisement)">Tag</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mountain_(advertisement)" title="Mountain (advertisement)">Mountain</a></i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Andrzej_Ciechanowiecki" title="Andrzej Ciechanowiecki">Andrzej Ciechanowiecki</a>, 91, Polish art historian.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mike_Davies_(tennis)" title="Mike Davies (tennis)">Mike Davies</a>, 79, Welsh tennis player, mesothelioma.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Roy_Dommett" title="Roy Dommett">Roy Dommett</a>, 82, British engineer and rocket scientist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Peter_Donaldson" title="Peter Donaldson">Peter Donaldson</a>, 70, Egyptian-born British newsreader and radio broadcaster (<a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_4" title="BBC Radio 4">BBC Radio 4</a>), cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Christopher_Duggan" title="Christopher Duggan">Christopher Duggan</a>, 57, British historian.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Omar_El-Hariri" title="Omar El-Hariri">Omar El-Hariri</a>, c. 71, Libyan general, traffic collision.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hashim_Abdul_Halim" title="Hashim Abdul Halim">Hashim Abdul Halim</a>, 80, Indian politician, <a href="/wiki/West_Bengal_Legislative_Assembly" title="West Bengal Legislative Assembly">West Bengal MLA</a> for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Amdanga" title="Amdanga">Amdanga</a> (1977–2006) and <a href="/wiki/Entally" title="Entally">Entally</a> (2006–2011), heart attack.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Karl_Jaeger_(educator)" title="Karl Jaeger (educator)">Karl Jaeger</a>, 85, American educator, writer and artist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Haruko_Kato" title="Haruko Kato">Haruko Kato</a>, 92, Japanese actress.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alexey_Kozlov_(intelligence_officer)" title="Alexey Kozlov (intelligence officer)">Alexey Kozlov</a>, 80, Russian Soviet intelligence officer, <a href="/wiki/Hero_of_the_Russian_Federation" title="Hero of the Russian Federation">Hero of the Russian Federation</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Neville_Lakay" title="Neville Lakay">Neville Lakay</a>, 77, South African cricketer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eddie_Milner" title="Eddie Milner">Eddie Milner</a>, 60, American baseball player (<a href="/wiki/Cincinnati_Reds" title="Cincinnati Reds">Cincinnati Reds</a>, <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_Giants" title="San Francisco Giants">San Francisco Giants</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tommy_Overstreet" title="Tommy Overstreet">Tommy Overstreet</a>, 78, American country singer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rom%C3%A9o_Phillion" title="Roméo Phillion">Roméo Phillion</a>, 76, Canadian prisoner, wrongly convicted of murder, COPD.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Miroslav_Poljak" title="Miroslav Poljak">Miroslav Poljak</a>, 71, Croatian water polo player, Olympic champion (<a href="/wiki/Water_polo_at_the_1968_Summer_Olympics" title="Water polo at the 1968 Summer Olympics">1968</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kondavalasa_Lakshmana_Rao" title="Kondavalasa Lakshmana Rao">Kondavalasa Lakshmana Rao</a>, 69, Indian actor, brain infection.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arthur_Shaw_(footballer,_born_1924)" title="Arthur Shaw (footballer, born 1924)">Arthur Shaw</a>, 91, English footballer (<a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Donald_Shell" title="Donald Shell">Donald Shell</a>, 91, American computer scientist (<a href="/wiki/Shellsort" title="Shellsort">Shellsort</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Barbara_Snelling" title="Barbara Snelling">Barbara Snelling</a>, 87, American politician, <a href="/wiki/Vermont" title="Vermont">Vermont</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_lieutenant_governors_of_Vermont" title="List of lieutenant governors of Vermont">Lieutenant Governor</a> (1993–1997), <a href="/wiki/Vermont_Senate" title="Vermont Senate">State Senator</a> (1999–2002), and First Lady (1977–1985 and 1991).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Edward_Soja" title="Edward Soja">Edward Soja</a>, 75, American geographer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Stock" title="David Stock">David Stock</a>, 76, American composer and conductor, blood disease.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Carlos_Vargas_Ferrer" title="Carlos Vargas Ferrer">Carlos Vargas Ferrer</a>, 44, Puerto Rican politician, member of the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Representatives_of_Puerto_Rico" title="House of Representatives of Puerto Rico">P.R. House of Representatives</a>, traffic collision following a heart attack.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Colin_Welland" title="Colin Welland">Colin Welland</a>, 81, British actor and screenwriter (<i><a href="/wiki/Kes_(film)" title="Kes (film)">Kes</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Straw_Dogs_(1971_film)" title="Straw Dogs (1971 film)">Straw Dogs</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Chariots_of_Fire" title="Chariots of Fire">Chariots of Fire</a></i>), <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Original_Screenplay" title="Academy Award for Best Original Screenplay">Oscar</a> winner (<a href="/wiki/54th_Academy_Awards" title="54th Academy Awards">1982</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/O%CA%BBtkir_Sultonov" title="Oʻtkir Sultonov">Oʻtkir Sultonov</a>, 76, Uzbek politician, <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Uzbekistan" title="Prime Minister of Uzbekistan">Prime Minister</a> (1995–2003).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-476"><a href="#cite_note-476">[476]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
